Find the values of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.439ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.138ex" height="1.439ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 503 636"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="70" d="M23 287Q24 290 25 295T30 317T40 348T55 381T75 411T101 433T134 442Q209 442 230 378L240 387Q302 442 358 442Q423 442 460 395T497 281Q497 173 421 82T249 -10Q227 -10 210 -4Q199 1 187 11T168 28L161 36Q160 35 139 -51T118 -138Q118 -144 126 -145T163 -148H188Q194 -155 194 -157T191 -175Q188 -187 185 -190T172 -194Q170 -194 161 -194T127 -193T65 -192Q-5 -192 -24 -194H-32Q-39 -187 -39 -183Q-37 -156 -26 -148H-6Q28 -147 33 -136Q36 -130 94 103T155 350Q156 355 156 364Q156 405 131 405Q109 405 94 377T71 316T59 280Q57 278 43 278H29Q23 284 23 287ZM178 102Q200 26 252 26Q282 26 310 49T356 107Q374 141 392 215T411 325V331Q411 405 350 405Q339 405 328 402T306 393T286 380T269 365T254 350T243 336T235 326L232 322Q232 321 229 308T218 264T204 212Q178 106 178 102Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.439ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.041ex" height="1.439ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 460 636"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="71" d="M33 157Q33 258 109 349T280 441Q340 441 372 389Q373 390 377 395T388 406T404 418Q438 442 450 442Q454 442 457 439T460 434Q460 425 391 149Q320 -135 320 -139Q320 -147 365 -148H390Q396 -156 396 -157T393 -175Q389 -188 383 -194H370Q339 -192 262 -192Q234 -192 211 -192T174 -192T157 -193Q143 -193 143 -185Q143 -182 145 -170Q149 -154 152 -151T172 -148Q220 -148 230 -141Q238 -136 258 -53T279 32Q279 33 272 29Q224 -10 172 -10Q117 -10 75 30T33 157ZM352 326Q329 405 277 405Q242 405 210 374T160 293Q131 214 119 129Q119 126 119 118T118 106Q118 61 136 44T179 26Q233 26 290 98L298 109L352 326Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Since it is moving with constant velocity, the net force is zero. Therefore, the sum of the forces must equal zero.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The forces are</div>

<div>For constant velocity the net force is zero, so</div>

<br>
<ol start="2">
<li>(a) Calculate the acceleration of an object of mass 150 kg subject to a net force of 60 N .</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Use Newtons second law, which states that the acceleration <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.197ex" height="1.02ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -441 529 451"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="61" d="M33 157Q33 258 109 349T280 441Q331 441 370 392Q386 422 416 422Q429 422 439 414T449 394Q449 381 412 234T374 68Q374 43 381 35T402 26Q411 27 422 35Q443 55 463 131Q469 151 473 152Q475 153 483 153H487Q506 153 506 144Q506 138 501 117T481 63T449 13Q436 0 417 -8Q409 -10 393 -10Q359 -10 336 5T306 36L300 51Q299 52 296 50Q294 48 292 46Q233 -10 172 -10Q117 -10 75 30T33 157ZM351 328Q351 334 346 350T323 385T277 405Q242 405 210 374T160 293Q131 214 119 129Q119 126 119 118T118 106Q118 61 136 44T179 26Q217 26 254 59T298 110Q300 114 325 217T351 328Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> of an object is given by the net force <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.695ex" height="1.538ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -680 749 680"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="46" d="M48 1Q31 1 31 11Q31 13 34 25Q38 41 42 43T65 46Q92 46 125 49Q139 52 144 61Q146 66 215 342T285 622Q285 629 281 629Q273 632 228 634H197Q191 640 191 642T193 659Q197 676 203 680H742Q749 676 749 669Q749 664 736 557T722 447Q720 440 702 440H690Q683 445 683 453Q683 454 686 477T689 530Q689 560 682 579T663 610T626 626T575 633T503 634H480Q398 633 393 631Q388 629 386 623Q385 622 352 492L320 363H375Q378 363 398 363T426 364T448 367T472 374T489 386Q502 398 511 419T524 457T529 475Q532 480 548 480H560Q567 475 567 470Q567 467 536 339T502 207Q500 200 482 200H470Q463 206 463 212Q463 215 468 234T473 274Q473 303 453 310T364 317H309L277 190Q245 66 245 60Q245 46 334 46H359Q365 40 365 39T363 19Q359 6 353 0H336Q295 2 185 2Q120 2 86 2T48 1Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> acting on it divided by its mass <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.986ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 878 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6D" d="M21 287Q22 293 24 303T36 341T56 388T88 425T132 442T175 435T205 417T221 395T229 376L231 369Q231 367 232 367L243 378Q303 442 384 442Q401 442 415 440T441 433T460 423T475 411T485 398T493 385T497 373T500 364T502 357L510 367Q573 442 659 442Q713 442 746 415T780 336Q780 285 742 178T704 50Q705 36 709 31T724 26Q752 26 776 56T815 138Q818 149 821 151T837 153Q857 153 857 145Q857 144 853 130Q845 101 831 73T785 17T716 -10Q669 -10 648 17T627 73Q627 92 663 193T700 345Q700 404 656 404H651Q565 404 506 303L499 291L466 157Q433 26 428 16Q415 -11 385 -11Q372 -11 364 -4T353 8T350 18Q350 29 384 161L420 307Q423 322 423 345Q423 404 379 404H374Q288 404 229 303L222 291L189 157Q156 26 151 16Q138 -11 108 -11Q95 -11 87 -5T76 7T74 17Q74 30 112 181Q151 335 151 342Q154 357 154 369Q154 405 129 405Q107 405 92 377T69 316T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>:</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
Using Newton's second law,
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -1.577ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="7.825ex" height="4.645ex" role="img" focusable="false" data-mml-node="mfrac" transform="translate(1862.6, 0)"><g data-mml-node="mi" transform="translate(284.5, 676)"><path data-c="46" d="M48 1Q31 1 31 11Q31 13 34 25Q38 41 42 43T65 46Q92 46 125 49Q139 52 <div>Therefore the acceleration is <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="8.768ex" height="1.937ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -833.9 3875.3 </div>
</details>
<br>
<div>(b) A load of mass 150 kg is accelerating vertically upwards as the result of the pull of a crane wire. The tension in the wire is 1488 N .<br>
Assuming that the only forces acting on the load are its weight and the tension in the wire, calculate the acceleration of the load.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Calculate the weight of the load first, then find the net force acting on the load. Finally, use Newtons second law to find the acceleration.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<div>The weight is</div>

<div>By Newtons second law, the acceleration is</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<br>
<ol start="3">
<li>A car of mass 1500 kg is pulling a trailer of mass 900 kg along a straight, horizontal road. The coupling between the car and the trailer is light, rigid and horizontal.</li>
</ol>
<div>The motion of the car and trailer is modelled assuming that the resistances to motion are negligible. There is a driving force of 600 N acting on the car.<br>
(a) Draw separate diagrams showing the horizontal force(s) acting on<br>
(i) the car.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<p align="center">
<img src="/assets/Mech1_Force_Q3.jpg" alt="drawing" width="500"/>
</p>
</div>
</details>
<br>
<div>(ii) the trailer.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<p align="center">
<img src="/assets/Mech1_Force_Q3.jpg" alt="drawing" width="500"/>
</p>
</div>
</details>
<br>
<div>(b) Calculate the acceleration of the car and trailer.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Use Newtons second law to find the acceleration of the combined mass of the car and trailer.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>Apply the Newtons second law to the whole system of car and trailer.</div>
<div>The total mass of the car and trailer is</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>Using Newtons second law, the acceleration is</div>

<div>Therefore the acceleration of the car and trailer is <span class="math-inline ">

</details>
<br>
<div>The situation is remodelled to include a constant resistant force of 150 N on the car and 100 N on the trailer.<br>
<span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.74ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 1211 1000"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mo"><path data-c="28" d="M94 250Q94 319 104 381T127 488T164 576T202 643T244 695T277 729T302 750H315H319Q333 750 333 741Q333 738 316 720T275 667T226 581T184 443T167 250T184 58T225 -81T274 -167T316 -220T333 -241Q333 -250 318 -250H315H302L274 -226Q180 -141 137 -14T94 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mi" transform="translate(389, 0)"><path data-c="63" d="M34 159Q34 268 120 355T306 442Q362 442 394 418T427 355Q427 326 408 306T360 285Q341 285 330 295T319 325T330 359T352 380T366 386H367Q367 388 361 392T340 400T306 404Q276 404 249 390Q228 381 206 359Q162 315 142 235T121 119Q121 73 147 50Q169 26 205 26H209Q321 26 394 111Q403 121 406 121Q410 121 419 112T429 98T420 83T391 55T346 25T282 0T202 -11Q127 -11 81 37T34 159Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(822, 0)"><path data-c="29" d="M60 749L64 750Q69 750 74 750H86L114 726Q208 641 251 514T294 250Q294 182 284 119T261 12T224 -76T186 -143T145 -194T113 -227T90 -246Q87 -249 86 -250H74Q66 -250 63 -250T58 -247T55 -238Q56 -237 66 -225Q221 -64 221 250T66 725Q56 737 55 738Q55 746 60 749Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> Find the tension in the coupling.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<p align="center">
<img src="/assets/Mech1_Force_Q3.jpg" alt="drawing" width="500"/>
</p>
<div>Again, use Newtons second law to find the acceleration of the combined mass of the car and trailer, taking into account the resistant forces. Then, use this acceleration to find the tension in the coupling by considering the forces acting on the trailer.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>We can use Newtons second law on whole system to find the acceleration first. Or we can focus on the forces acting on the car or trailer. Here we use the the trailer.</div>
<div>The total resistant force is</div>

<div>The net force acting on the car and trailer is</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.357ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="25.033ex" height="1.902ex" role="img" focusable="false" <div>Using Newtons second law, the acceleration is</div>

<div>The forces acting on the trailer are the tension <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.593ex" height="1.532ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -677 704 677"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M40 437Q21 437 21 445Q21 450 37 501T71 602L88 651Q93 669 101 677H569H659Q691 677 697 676T704 667Q704 661 687 553T668 444Q668 437 649 437Q640 437 637 437T631 442L629 445Q629 451 635 490T641 551Q641 586 628 604T573 629Q568 630 515 631Q469 631 457 630T439 622Q438 621 368 343T298 60Q298 48 386 46Q418 46 427 45T436 36Q436 31 433 22Q429 4 424 1L422 0Q419 0 415 0Q410 0 363 1T228 2Q99 2 64 0H49Q43 6 43 9T45 27Q49 40 55 46H83H94Q174 46 189 55Q190 56 191 56Q196 59 201 76T241 233Q258 301 269 344Q339 619 339 625Q339 630 310 630H279Q212 630 191 624Q146 614 121 583T67 467Q60 445 57 441T43 437H40Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> in the coupling and the resistant force of 100 N. Using Newtons second law for the trailer,</div>

<div>Solving for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.593ex" height="1.532ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -677 704 677"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M40 437Q21 437 21 445Q21 450 37 501T71 602L88 651Q93 669 101 677H569H659Q691 677 697 676T704 667Q704 661 687 553T668 444Q668 437 649 437Q640 437 637 437T631 442L629 445Q629 451 635 490T641 551Q641 586 628 604T573 629Q568 630 515 631Q469 631 457 630T439 622Q438 621 368 343T298 60Q298 48 386 46Q418 46 427 45T436 36Q436 31 433 22Q429 4 424 1L422 0Q419 0 415 0Q410 0 363 1T228 2Q99 2 64 0H49Q43 6 43 9T45 27Q49 40 55 46H83H94Q174 46 189 55Q190 56 191 56Q196 59 201 76T241 233Q258 301 269 344Q339 619 339 625Q339 630 310 630H279Q212 630 191 624Q146 614 121 583T67 467Q60 445 57 441T43 437H40Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>,</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -1.602ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="34.631ex" height="4.638ex" role="img" focusable="false" <li>In this question, the unit vector <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.722ex" height="1.572ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -695 319 695"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="69" d="M72 610Q72 649 98 672T159 695Q193 693 217 670T241 610Q241 572 217 549T157 525Q120 525 96 548T72 610ZM46 442L136 446L226 450H232V62H294V0H286Q271 3 171 3Q67 3 49 0H40V62H109V209Q109 358 108 362Q103 380 55 380H43V442H46Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is horizontal and the unit vector <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.452ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.794ex" height="2.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -695 351 895"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6A" d="M104 610Q104 649 130 672T191 695Q225 693 249 670T273 610Q273 572 249 549T189 525Q152 525 128 548T104 610ZM78 442L173 446L268 450H274V196Q274 -5 274 -37T269 -83Q256 -132 201 -166T71 -200Q10 -200 -30 -173T-71 -102Q-71 -70 -51 -51T-1 -31Q27 -31 48 -49T69 -100Q69 -121 53 -147H56Q66 -149 77 -149H80Q90 -149 100 -146T127 -125T149 -73Q151 -55 151 149V362Q150 364 148 366T145 370T142 373T138 375T133 377T124 378T113 379T97 380H75V442H78Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is vertically upwards. All forces are in Newtons.<br>
A small, heavy box is suspended in mid-air and is held in equilibrium by the tension in a light inextensible string and a horizontal force, as shown in the diagram.<br>

The horizontal force is <span class="math-inline ">

(a) Find the value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.439ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.138ex" height="1.439ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 503 636"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="70" d="M23 287Q24 290 25 295T30 317T40 348T55 381T75 411T101 433T134 442Q209 442 230 378L240 387Q302 442 358 442Q423 442 460 395T497 281Q497 173 421 82T249 -10Q227 -10 210 -4Q199 1 187 11T168 28L161 36Q160 35 139 -51T118 -138Q118 -144 126 -145T163 -148H188Q194 -155 194 -157T191 -175Q188 -187 185 -190T172 -194Q170 -194 161 -194T127 -193T65 -192Q-5 -192 -24 -194H-32Q-39 -187 -39 -183Q-37 -156 -26 -148H-6Q28 -147 33 -136Q36 -130 94 103T155 350Q156 355 156 364Q156 405 131 405Q109 405 94 377T71 316T59 280Q57 278 43 278H29Q23 284 23 287ZM178 102Q200 26 252 26Q282 26 310 49T356 107Q374 141 392 215T411 325V331Q411 405 350 405Q339 405 328 402T306 393T286 380T269 365T254 350T243 336T235 326L232 322Q232 321 229 308T218 264T204 212Q178 106 178 102Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>All forces acting on the box must sum to zero since it is in equilibrium. Therefore, the sum of the horizontal components of the forces must equal zero.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The forces acting on the box are the tension <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.723ex" height="1.867ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -675 1203.6 825"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M41 425Q41 426 51 545T62 669V675H737V669Q738 665 748 546T758 425V419H696V425Q687 517 669 555T595 607Q578 612 522 613H478V62H631V0H615Q585 3 399 3Q214 3 184 0H168V62H321V613H277H263Q164 613 134 561Q113 527 103 425V419H41V425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(800, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and the horizontal force <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.551ex" height="1.878ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -680 1127.6 830"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="46" d="M425 0L228 3Q63 3 51 0H39V62H147V618H39V680H644V676Q647 670 659 552T675 428V424H613Q613 433 605 477Q599 511 589 535T562 574T530 599T488 612T441 617T387 618H368H304V371H333Q389 373 411 390T437 468V488H499V192H437V212Q436 244 430 263T408 292T378 305T333 309H304V62H439V0H425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(724, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. Since the box is in equilibrium, the sum of the forces must equal zero:<br>
<span class="math-block ">

where <span class="math-inline ">

The horizontal components give:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>Solving for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.439ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.138ex" height="1.439ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 503 636"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="70" d="M23 287Q24 290 25 295T30 317T40 348T55 381T75 411T101 433T134 442Q209 442 230 378L240 387Q302 442 358 442Q423 442 460 395T497 281Q497 173 421 82T249 -10Q227 -10 210 -4Q199 1 187 11T168 28L161 36Q160 35 139 -51T118 -138Q118 -144 126 -145T163 -148H188Q194 -155 194 -157T191 -175Q188 -187 185 -190T172 -194Q170 -194 161 -194T127 -193T65 -192Q-5 -192 -24 -194H-32Q-39 -187 -39 -183Q-37 -156 -26 -148H-6Q28 -147 33 -136Q36 -130 94 103T155 350Q156 355 156 364Q156 405 131 405Q109 405 94 377T71 316T59 280Q57 278 43 278H29Q23 284 23 287ZM178 102Q200 26 252 26Q282 26 310 49T356 107Q374 141 392 215T411 325V331Q411 405 350 405Q339 405 328 402T306 393T286 380T269 365T254 350T243 336T235 326L232 322Q232 321 229 308T218 264T204 212Q178 106 178 102Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> gives:<br>

Therefore, the value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.439ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.138ex" height="1.439ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 503 636"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="70" d="M23 287Q24 290 25 295T30 317T40 348T55 381T75 411T101 433T134 442Q209 442 230 378L240 387Q302 442 358 442Q423 442 460 395T497 281Q497 173 421 82T249 -10Q227 -10 210 -4Q199 1 187 11T168 28L161 36Q160 35 139 -51T118 -138Q118 -144 126 -145T163 -148H188Q194 -155 194 -157T191 -175Q188 -187 185 -190T172 -194Q170 -194 161 -194T127 -193T65 -192Q-5 -192 -24 -194H-32Q-39 -187 -39 -183Q-37 -156 -26 -148H-6Q28 -147 33 -136Q36 -130 94 103T155 350Q156 355 156 364Q156 405 131 405Q109 405 94 377T71 316T59 280Q57 278 43 278H29Q23 284 23 287ZM178 102Q200 26 252 26Q282 26 310 49T356 107Q374 141 392 215T411 325V331Q411 405 350 405Q339 405 328 402T306 393T286 380T269 365T254 350T243 336T235 326L232 322Q232 321 229 308T218 264T204 212Q178 106 178 102Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.023ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 1778 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mo"><path data-c="2212" d="M84 237T84 250T98 270H679Q694 262 694 250T679 230H98Q84 237 84 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(778, 0)"><path data-c="33" d="M127 463Q100 463 85 480T69 524Q69 579 117 622T233 665Q268 665 277 664Q351 652 390 611T430 522Q430 470 396 421T302 350L299 348Q299 347 308 345T337 336T375 315Q457 262 457 175Q457 96 395 37T238 -22Q158 -22 100 21T42 130Q42 158 60 175T105 193Q133 193 151 175T169 130Q169 119 166 110T159 94T148 82T136 74T126 70T118 67L114 66Q165 21 238 21Q293 21 321 74Q338 107 338 175V195Q338 290 274 322Q259 328 213 329L171 330L168 332Q166 335 166 348Q166 366 174 366Q202 366 232 371Q266 376 294 413T322 525V533Q322 590 287 612Q265 626 240 626Q208 626 181 615T143 592T132 580H135Q138 579 143 578T153 573T165 566T175 555T183 540T186 520Q186 498 172 481T127 463Z"></path><path data-c="30" d="M96 585Q152 666 249 666Q297 666 345 640T423 548Q460 465 460 320Q460 165 417 83Q397 41 362 16T301 -15T250 -22Q224 -22 198 -16T137 16T82 83Q39 165 39 320Q39 494 96 585ZM321 597Q291 629 250 629Q208 629 178 597Q153 571 145 525T137 333Q137 175 145 125T181 46Q209 16 250 16Q290 16 318 46Q347 76 354 130T362 333Q362 478 354 524T321 597Z" transform="translate(500, 0)"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
</div>
</details>
<br>
<div>(b) Find the mass <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.986ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 878 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6D" d="M21 287Q22 293 24 303T36 341T56 388T88 425T132 442T175 435T205 417T221 395T229 376L231 369Q231 367 232 367L243 378Q303 442 384 442Q401 442 415 440T441 433T460 423T475 411T485 398T493 385T497 373T500 364T502 357L510 367Q573 442 659 442Q713 442 746 415T780 336Q780 285 742 178T704 50Q705 36 709 31T724 26Q752 26 776 56T815 138Q818 149 821 151T837 153Q857 153 857 145Q857 144 853 130Q845 101 831 73T785 17T716 -10Q669 -10 648 17T627 73Q627 92 663 193T700 345Q700 404 656 404H651Q565 404 506 303L499 291L466 157Q433 26 428 16Q415 -11 385 -11Q372 -11 364 -4T353 8T350 18Q350 29 384 161L420 307Q423 322 423 345Q423 404 379 404H374Q288 404 229 303L222 291L189 157Q156 26 151 16Q138 -11 108 -11Q95 -11 87 -5T76 7T74 17Q74 30 112 181Q151 335 151 342Q154 357 154 369Q154 405 129 405Q107 405 92 377T69 316T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>The vertical components of the forces must also sum to zero. Use this to find the weight of the box, and then use the weight to find the mass.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>

Solving for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.371ex" height="1.595ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 1048 705"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="57" d="M436 683Q450 683 486 682T553 680Q604 680 638 681T677 682Q695 682 695 674Q695 670 692 659Q687 641 683 639T661 637Q636 636 621 632T600 624T597 615Q597 603 613 377T629 138L631 141Q633 144 637 151T649 170T666 200T690 241T720 295T759 362Q863 546 877 572T892 604Q892 619 873 628T831 637Q817 637 817 647Q817 650 819 660Q823 676 825 679T839 682Q842 682 856 682T895 682T949 681Q1015 681 1034 683Q1048 683 1048 672Q1048 666 1045 655T1038 640T1028 637Q1006 637 988 631T958 617T939 600T927 584L923 578L754 282Q586 -14 585 -15Q579 -22 561 -22Q546 -22 542 -17Q539 -14 523 229T506 480L494 462Q472 425 366 239Q222 -13 220 -15T215 -19Q210 -22 197 -22Q178 -22 176 -15Q176 -12 154 304T131 622Q129 631 121 633T82 637H58Q51 644 51 648Q52 671 64 683H76Q118 680 176 680Q301 680 313 683H323Q329 677 329 674T327 656Q322 641 318 637H297Q236 634 232 620Q262 160 266 136L501 550L499 587Q496 629 489 632Q483 636 447 637Q428 637 422 639T416 648Q416 650 418 660Q419 664 420 669T421 676T424 680T428 682T436 683Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> gives:<br>

The weight is related to the mass <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.986ex" height="1.025ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 878 453"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="6D" d="M21 287Q22 293 24 303T36 341T56 388T88 425T132 442T175 435T205 417T221 395T229 376L231 369Q231 367 232 367L243 378Q303 442 384 442Q401 442 415 440T441 433T460 423T475 411T485 398T493 385T497 373T500 364T502 357L510 367Q573 442 659 442Q713 442 746 415T780 336Q780 285 742 178T704 50Q705 36 709 31T724 26Q752 26 776 56T815 138Q818 149 821 151T837 153Q857 153 857 145Q857 144 853 130Q845 101 831 73T785 17T716 -10Q669 -10 648 17T627 73Q627 92 663 193T700 345Q700 404 656 404H651Q565 404 506 303L499 291L466 157Q433 26 428 16Q415 -11 385 -11Q372 -11 364 -4T353 8T350 18Q350 29 384 161L420 307Q423 322 423 345Q423 404 379 404H374Q288 404 229 303L222 291L189 157Q156 26 151 16Q138 -11 108 -11Q95 -11 87 -5T76 7T74 17Q74 30 112 181Q151 335 151 342Q154 357 154 369Q154 405 129 405Q107 405 92 377T69 316T57 280Q55 278 41 278H27Q21 284 21 287Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> by the equation:<br>
<span class="math-block ">

where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.464ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.079ex" height="1.464ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -442 477 647"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="67" d="M311 43Q296 30 267 15T206 0Q143 0 105 45T66 160Q66 265 143 353T314 442Q361 442 401 394L404 398Q406 401 409 404T418 412T431 419T447 422Q461 422 470 413T480 394Q480 379 423 152T363 -80Q345 -134 286 -169T151 -205Q10 -205 10 -137Q10 -111 28 -91T74 -71Q89 -71 102 -80T116 -111Q116 -121 114 -130T107 -144T99 -154T92 -162L90 -164H91Q101 -167 151 -167Q189 -167 211 -155Q234 -144 254 -122T282 -75Q288 -56 298 -13Q311 35 311 43ZM384 328L380 339Q377 350 375 354T369 368T359 382T346 393T328 402T306 405Q262 405 221 352Q191 313 171 233T151 117Q151 38 213 38Q269 38 323 108L331 118L384 328Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the acceleration due to gravity, approximately <span class="math-inline ">

<div><span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.74ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 1211 1000"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mo"><path data-c="28" d="M94 250Q94 319 104 381T127 488T164 576T202 643T244 695T277 729T302 750H315H319Q333 750 333 741Q333 738 316 720T275 667T226 581T184 443T167 250T184 58T225 -81T274 -167T316 -220T333 -241Q333 -250 318 -250H315H302L274 -226Q180 -141 137 -14T94 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mi" transform="translate(389, 0)"><path data-c="63" d="M34 159Q34 268 120 355T306 442Q362 442 394 418T427 355Q427 326 408 306T360 285Q341 285 330 295T319 325T330 359T352 380T366 386H367Q367 388 361 392T340 400T306 404Q276 404 249 390Q228 381 206 359Q162 315 142 235T121 119Q121 73 147 50Q169 26 205 26H209Q321 26 394 111Q403 121 406 121Q410 121 419 112T429 98T420 83T391 55T346 25T282 0T202 -11Q127 -11 81 37T34 159Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(822, 0)"><path data-c="29" d="M60 749L64 750Q69 750 74 750H86L114 726Q208 641 251 514T294 250Q294 182 284 119T261 12T224 -76T186 -143T145 -194T113 -227T90 -246Q87 -249 86 -250H74Q66 -250 63 -250T58 -247T55 -238Q56 -237 66 -225Q221 -64 221 250T66 725Q56 737 55 738Q55 746 60 749Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> Calculate the magnitude of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.723ex" height="1.867ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -675 1203.6 825"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M41 425Q41 426 51 545T62 669V675H737V669Q738 665 748 546T758 425V419H696V425Q687 517 669 555T595 607Q578 612 522 613H478V62H631V0H615Q585 3 399 3Q214 3 184 0H168V62H321V613H277H263Q164 613 134 561Q113 527 103 425V419H41V425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(800, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and the angle that <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.723ex" height="1.867ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -675 1203.6 825"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M41 425Q41 426 51 545T62 669V675H737V669Q738 665 748 546T758 425V419H696V425Q687 517 669 555T595 607Q578 612 522 613H478V62H631V0H615Q585 3 399 3Q214 3 184 0H168V62H321V613H277H263Q164 613 134 561Q113 527 103 425V419H41V425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(800, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> makes with the horizontal.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Use the Pythagorean theorem to find the magnitude of the tension vector. To find the angle, use the tangent function.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The magnitude of the tension vector <span class="math-inline ">

The angle <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.061ex" height="1.618ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 469 715"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="3B8" d="M35 200Q35 302 74 415T180 610T319 704Q320 704 327 704T339 705Q393 701 423 656Q462 596 462 495Q462 380 417 261T302 66T168 -10H161Q125 -10 99 10T60 63T41 130T35 200ZM383 566Q383 668 330 668Q294 668 260 623T204 521T170 421T157 371Q206 370 254 370L351 371Q352 372 359 404T375 484T383 566ZM113 132Q113 26 166 26Q181 26 198 36T239 74T287 161T335 307L340 324H145Q145 321 136 286T120 208T113 132Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> that <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.723ex" height="1.867ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -675 1203.6 825"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M41 425Q41 426 51 545T62 669V675H737V669Q738 665 748 546T758 425V419H696V425Q687 517 669 555T595 607Q578 612 522 613H478V62H631V0H615Q585 3 399 3Q214 3 184 0H168V62H321V613H277H263Q164 613 134 561Q113 527 103 425V419H41V425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(800, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> makes with the horizontal can be found using the tangent function:<br>

Solving for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.061ex" height="1.618ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -705 469 715"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="3B8" d="M35 200Q35 302 74 415T180 610T319 704Q320 704 327 704T339 705Q393 701 423 656Q462 596 462 495Q462 380 417 261T302 66T168 -10H161Q125 -10 99 10T60 63T41 130T35 200ZM383 566Q383 668 330 668Q294 668 260 623T204 521T170 421T157 371Q206 370 254 370L351 371Q352 372 359 404T375 484T383 566ZM113 132Q113 26 166 26Q181 26 198 36T239 74T287 161T335 307L340 324H145Q145 321 136 286T120 208T113 132Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> gives:<br>

Therefore, the magnitude of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.723ex" height="1.867ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -675 1203.6 825"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M41 425Q41 426 51 545T62 669V675H737V669Q738 665 748 546T758 425V419H696V425Q687 517 669 555T595 607Q578 612 522 613H478V62H631V0H615Q585 3 399 3Q214 3 184 0H168V62H321V613H277H263Q164 613 134 561Q113 527 103 425V419H41V425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(800, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is approximately <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.05ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="7.416ex" height="1.595ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 3278 705"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="35" d="M164 157Q164 133 148 117T109 101H102Q148 22 224 22Q294 22 326 82Q345 115 345 210Q345 313 318 349Q292 382 260 382H254Q176 382 136 314Q132 307 129 306T114 304Q97 304 95 310Q93 314 93 485V614Q93 664 98 664Q100 666 102 666Q103 666 123 658T178 642T253 634Q324 634 389 662Q397 666 402 666Q410 666 410 648V635Q328 538 205 538Q174 538 149 544L139 546V374Q158 388 169 396T205 412T256 420Q337 420 393 355T449 201Q449 109 385 44T229 <summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Since the box is still in equilibrium, the sum of all forces acting on it must equal zero. Set up equations for the horizontal and vertical components of the forces and solve for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.197ex" height="1.02ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -441 529 451"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="61" d="M33 157Q33 258 109 349T280 441Q331 441 370 392Q386 422 416 422Q429 422 439 414T449 394Q449 381 412 234T374 68Q374 43 381 35T402 26Q411 27 422 35Q443 55 463 131Q469 151 473 152Q475 153 483 153H487Q506 153 506 144Q506 138 501 117T481 63T449 13Q436 0 417 -8Q409 -10 393 -10Q359 -10 336 5T306 36L300 51Q299 52 296 50Q294 48 292 46Q233 -10 172 -10Q117 -10 75 30T33 157ZM351 328Q351 334 346 350T323 385T277 405Q242 405 210 374T160 293Q131 214 119 129Q119 126 119 118T118 106Q118 61 136 44T179 26Q217 26 254 59T298 110Q300 114 325 217T351 328Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.971ex" height="1.595ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -694 429 705"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="62" d="M73 647Q73 657 77 670T89 683Q90 683 161 688T234 694Q246 694 246 685T212 542Q204 508 195 472T180 418L176 399Q176 396 182 402Q231 442 283 442Q345 442 383 396T422 280Q422 169 343 79T173 -11Q123 -11 82 27T40 150V159Q40 180 48 217T97 414Q147 611 147 623T109 637Q104 637 101 637H96Q86 637 83 637T76 640T73 647ZM336 325V331Q336 405 275 405Q258 405 240 397T207 376T181 352T163 330L157 322L136 236Q114 150 114 114Q114 66 138 42Q154 26 178 26Q211 26 245 58Q270 81 285 114T318 219Q336 291 336 325Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>

<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The forces acting on the box are now the tension <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.723ex" height="1.867ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -675 1203.6 825"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M41 425Q41 426 51 545T62 669V675H737V669Q738 665 748 546T758 425V419H696V425Q687 517 669 555T595 607Q578 612 522 613H478V62H631V0H615Q585 3 399 3Q214 3 184 0H168V62H321V613H277H263Q164 613 134 561Q113 527 103 425V419H41V425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(800, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>, the horizontal force <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.551ex" height="1.878ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -680 1127.6 830"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="46" d="M425 0L228 3Q63 3 51 0H39V62H147V618H39V680H644V676Q647 670 659 552T675 428V424H613Q613 433 605 477Q599 511 589 535T562 574T530 599T488 612T441 617T387 618H368H304V371H333Q389 373 411 390T437 468V488H499V192H437V212Q436 244 430 263T408 292T378 305T333 309H304V62H439V0H425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(724, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>, and the new force <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.339ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.551ex" height="1.878ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -680 1127.6 830"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msub"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="46" d="M425 0L228 3Q63 3 51 0H39V62H147V618H39V680H644V676Q647 670 659 552T675 428V424H613Q613 433 605 477Q599 511 589 535T562 574T530 599T488 612T441 617T387 618H368H304V371H333Q389 373 411 390T437 468V488H499V192H437V212Q436 244 430 263T408 292T378 305T333 309H304V62H439V0H425Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" transform="translate(724, -150) scale(0.707)" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mn"><path data-c="32" d="M109 429Q82 429 66 447T50 491Q50 562 103 614T235 666Q326 666 387 610T449 465Q449 422 429 383T381 315T301 241Q265 210 201 149L142 93L218 92Q375 92 385 97Q392 99 409 186V189H449V186Q448 183 436 95T421 3V0H50V19V31Q50 38 56 46T86 81Q115 113 136 137Q145 147 170 174T204 211T233 244T261 278T284 308T305 340T320 369T333 401T340 431T343 464Q343 527 309 573T212 619Q179 619 154 602T119 569T109 550Q109 549 114 549Q132 549 151 535T170 489Q170 464 154 447T109 429Z"></path></g></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. Since the box is in equilibrium, the sum of the forces must equal zero:<br>

where <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.016ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.69ex" height="1.568ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -686 1189 693"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="57" d="M915 686L1052 683Q1142 683 1157 686H1164V624H1073L957 320Q930 249 900 170T855 52T839 10Q834 0 826 -5Q821 -7 799 -7H792Q777 -7 772 -5T759 10Q759 11 748 39T716 122T676 228L594 442L512 228Q486 159 455 78Q433 19 428 9T416 -5Q411 -7 389 -7H379Q356 -7 349 10Q349 12 334 51T288 170T231 320L116 624H24V686H35Q44 683 183 683Q331 683 355 686H368V624H323Q278 624 278 623L437 207L499 369L561 531L526 624H434V686H445Q454 683 593 683Q741 683 765 686H778V624H733Q688 624 688 623L847 207Q848 207 927 415T1006 624H905V686H915Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> is the weight of the box acting vertically downwards.<br>

Solving for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.197ex" height="1.02ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -441 529 451"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="61" d="M33 157Q33 258 109 349T280 441Q331 441 370 392Q386 422 416 422Q429 422 439 414T449 394Q449 381 412 234T374 68Q374 43 381 35T402 26Q411 27 422 35Q443 55 463 131Q469 151 473 152Q475 153 483 153H487Q506 153 506 144Q506 138 501 117T481 63T449 13Q436 0 417 -8Q409 -10 393 -10Q359 -10 336 5T306 36L300 51Q299 52 296 50Q294 48 292 46Q233 -10 172 -10Q117 -10 75 30T33 157ZM351 328Q351 334 346 350T323 385T277 405Q242 405 210 374T160 293Q131 214 119 129Q119 126 119 118T118 106Q118 61 136 44T179 26Q217 26 254 59T298 110Q300 114 325 217T351 328Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> gives:<br>
<span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="8.237ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" The vertical components give:<br>

Solving for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.025ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="0.971ex" height="1.595ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -694 429 705"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="62" d="M73 647Q73 657 77 670T89 683Q90 683 161 688T234 694Q246 694 246 685T212 542Q204 508 195 472T180 418L176 399Q176 396 182 402Q231 442 283 442Q345 442 383 396T422 280Q422 169 343 79T173 -11Q123 -11 82 27T40 150V159Q40 180 48 217T97 414Q147 611 147 623T109 637Q104 637 101 637H96Q86 637 83 637T76 640T73 647ZM336 325V331Q336 405 275 405Q258 405 240 397T207 376T181 352T163 330L157 322L136 236Q114 150 114 114Q114 66 138 42Q154 26 178 26Q211 26 245 58Q270 81 285 114T318 219Q336 291 336 325Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> gives:<br>
<span class="math-block ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG" display="true"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="6.25ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 Therefore, the values of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.197ex" height="1.02ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -441 529 451"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="61" d="M33 157Q33 258 109 349T280 441Q331 441 370 392Q386 422 416 422Q429 422 439 414T449 394Q449 381 412 234T374 68Q374 43 381 35T402 26Q411 27 422 35Q443 55 463 131Q469 151 473 152Q475 153 483 153H487Q506 153 506 144Q506 138 501 117T481 63T449 13Q436 0 417 -8Q409 -10 393 -10Q359 -10 336 5T306 36L300 51Q299 52 296 50Q294 48 292 46Q233 -10 172 -10Q117 -10 75 30T33 157ZM351 328Q351 334 346 350T323 385T277 405Q242 405 210 374T160 293Q131 214 119 129Q119 126 119 118T118 106Q118 61 136 44T179 26Q217 26 254 59T298 110Q300 114 325 217T351 328Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">

<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.186ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.023ex" height="1.692ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -666 1778 748"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mo"><path data-c="2212" d="M84 237T84 250T98 270H679Q694 262 694 250T679 230H98Q84 237 84 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mn" transform="translate(778, 0)"><path data-c="31" d="M213 578L200 573Q186 568 160 563T102 556H83V602H102Q149 604 189 617T245 641T273 663Q275 666 285 666Q294 666 302 660V361L303 61Q310 54 315 52T339 48T401 46H427V0H416Q395 3 257 3Q121 3 100 0H88V46H114Q136 46 152 46T177 47T193 50T201 52T207 57T213 61V578Z"></path><path data-c="38" d="M70 417T70 494T124 618T248 666Q319 666 374 624T429 515Q429 485 418 459T392 417T361 389T335 371T324 363L338 354Q352 344 366 334T382 323Q457 264 457 174Q457 95 399 37T249 -22Q159 -22 101 29T43 155Q43 263 172 335L154 348Q133 361 127 368Q70 417 70 494ZM286 386L292 390Q298 394 301 396T311 403T323 413T334 425T345 438T355 454T364 471T369 491T371 513Q371 556 342 586T275 624Q268 625 242 625Q201 625 165 599T128 534Q128 511 141 492T167 463T217 431Q224 426 228 424L286 386ZM250 21Q308 21 350 55T392 137Q392 154 387 169T375 194T353 216T330 234T301 253T274 270Q260 279 244 289T218 306L210 311Q204 311 181 294T133 239T107 157Q107 98 150 60T250 21Z" transform="translate(500, 0)"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and <span class="math-inline ">

The normal reaction of the floor of the lift on the girl is <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.048ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="3.98ex" height="1.593ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 1759 704"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="52" d="M230 637Q203 637 198 638T193 649Q193 676 204 682Q206 683 378 683Q550 682 564 680Q620 672 658 652T712 606T733 563T739 529Q739 484 710 445T643 385T576 351T538 338L545 333Q612 295 612 223Q612 212 607 162T602 80V71Q602 53 603 43T614 25T640 16Q668 16 686 38T712 85Q717 99 720 102T735 105Q755 105 755 93Q755 75 731 36Q693 -21 641 -21H632Q571 -21 531 4T487 82Q487 109 502 166T517 239Q517 290 474 313Q459 320 449 321T378 323H309L277 193Q244 61 244 59Q244 55 245 54T252 50T269 48T302 46H333Q339 38 339 37T336 19Q332 6 326 0H311Q275 2 180 2Q146 2 117 2T71 2T50 1Q33 1 33 10Q33 12 36 24Q41 43 46 45Q50 46 61 46H67Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628Q287 635 230 637ZM630 554Q630 586 609 608T523 636Q521 636 500 636T462 637H440Q393 637 386 627Q385 624 352 494T319 361Q319 360 388 360Q466 361 492 367Q556 377 592 426Q608 449 619 486T630 554Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD" transform="translate(759, 0)"><g data-mml-node="mtext"><path data-c="A0" d=""></path></g><g data-mml-node="mi" transform="translate(250, 0)"><path data-c="4E" d="M42 46Q74 48 94 56T118 69T128 86V634H124Q114 637 52 637H25V683H232L235 680Q237 679 322 554T493 303L578 178V598Q572 608 568 613T544 627T492 637H475V683H483Q498 680 600 680Q706 680 715 683H724V637H707Q634 633 622 598L621 302V6L614 0H600Q585 0 582 3T481 150T282 443T171 605V345L172 86Q183 50 257 46H274V0H265Q250 3 150 3Q48 3 33 0H25V46H42Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
(a) Find the minimum value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.048ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.717ex" height="1.593ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 759 704"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="52" d="M230 637Q203 637 198 638T193 649Q193 676 204 682Q206 683 378 683Q550 682 564 680Q620 672 658 652T712 606T733 563T739 529Q739 484 710 445T643 385T576 351T538 338L545 333Q612 295 612 223Q612 212 607 162T602 80V71Q602 53 603 43T614 25T640 16Q668 16 686 38T712 85Q717 99 720 102T735 105Q755 105 755 93Q755 75 731 36Q693 -21 641 -21H632Q571 -21 531 4T487 82Q487 109 502 166T517 239Q517 290 474 313Q459 320 449 321T378 323H309L277 193Q244 61 244 59Q244 55 245 54T252 50T269 48T302 46H333Q339 38 339 37T336 19Q332 6 326 0H311Q275 2 180 2Q146 2 117 2T71 2T50 1Q33 1 33 10Q33 12 36 24Q41 43 46 45Q50 46 61 46H67Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628Q287 635 230 637ZM630 554Q630 586 609 608T523 636Q521 636 500 636T462 637H440Q393 637 386 627Q385 624 352 494T319 361Q319 360 388 360Q466 361 492 367Q556 377 592 426Q608 449 619 486T630 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> during the motion.</li>
</ol>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
Consider the different phases of the lift's motion: acceleration, constant speed, and deceleration. The minimum value of $R$ will occur during the deceleration phase. Use Newton's second law to find $R$ during this phase.
Thw
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">

<div>The minimum value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.048ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.717ex" height="1.593ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 759 704"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="52" d="M230 637Q203 637 198 638T193 649Q193 676 204 682Q206 683 378 683Q550 682 564 680Q620 672 658 652T712 606T733 563T739 529Q739 484 710 445T643 385T576 351T538 338L545 333Q612 295 612 223Q612 212 607 162T602 80V71Q602 53 603 43T614 25T640 16Q668 16 686 38T712 85Q717 99 720 102T735 105Q755 105 755 93Q755 75 731 36Q693 -21 641 -21H632Q571 -21 531 4T487 82Q487 109 502 166T517 239Q517 290 474 313Q459 320 449 321T378 323H309L277 193Q244 61 244 59Q244 55 245 54T252 50T269 48T302 46H333Q339 38 339 37T336 19Q332 6 326 0H311Q275 2 180 2Q146 2 117 2T71 2T50 1Q33 1 33 10Q33 12 36 24Q41 43 46 45Q50 46 61 46H67Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628Q287 635 230 637ZM630 554Q630 586 609 608T523 636Q521 636 500 636T462 637H440Q393 637 386 627Q385 624 352 494T319 361Q319 360 388 360Q466 361 492 367Q556 377 592 426Q608 449 619 486T630 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> occurs during the deceleration phase, which is <span class="math-inline ">

<br>
<div>(b) Given that the string does not break during the motion, find the maximum tension in the string during the motion.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>The maximum tension in the string will occur during the acceleration phase of the lifts motion. Use Newtons second law to find the tension during this phase.<br>
Similarly, calculate the tension during constant speed and deceleration phases to confirm the maximum value.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>Calculate the tension <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.593ex" height="1.532ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -677 704 677"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="54" d="M40 437Q21 437 21 445Q21 450 37 501T71 602L88 651Q93 669 101 677H569H659Q691 677 697 676T704 667Q704 661 687 553T668 444Q668 437 649 437Q640 437 637 437T631 442L629 445Q629 451 635 490T641 551Q641 586 628 604T573 629Q568 630 515 631Q469 631 457 630T439 622Q438 621 368 343T298 60Q298 48 386 46Q418 46 427 45T436 36Q436 31 433 22Q429 4 424 1L422 0Q419 0 415 0Q410 0 363 1T228 2Q99 2 64 0H49Q43 6 43 9T45 27Q49 40 55 46H83H94Q174 46 189 55Q190 56 191 56Q196 59 201 76T241 233Q258 301 269 344Q339 619 339 625Q339 630 310 630H279Q212 630 191 624Q146 614 121 583T67 467Q60 445 57 441T43 437H40Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> in the string during each phase of the lifts motion.</div>

2. During constant speed (<span class="math-inline ">

<li>Three particles, <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.439ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="4.305ex" height="2.059ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -716 1902.7 910"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="41" d="M255 0Q240 3 140 3Q48 3 39 0H32V46H47Q119 49 139 88Q140 91 192 245T295 553T348 708Q351 716 366 716H376Q396 715 400 709Q402 707 508 390L617 67Q624 54 636 51T687 46H717V0H708Q699 3 581 3Q458 3 437 0H427V46H440Q510 46 510 64Q510 66 486 138L462 209H229L209 150Q189 91 189 85Q189 72 209 59T259 46H264V0H255ZM447 255L345 557L244 256Q244 255 345 255H447Z"></path></g></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(750, 0)"><path data-c="2C" d="M78 35T78 60T94 103T137 121Q165 121 187 96T210 8Q210 -27 201 -60T180 -117T154 -158T130 -185T117 -194Q113 -194 104 -185T95 -172Q95 -168 106 -156T131 -126T157 -76T173 -3V9L172 8Q170 7 167 6T161 3T152 1T140 0Q113 0 96 17Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="TeXAtom" data-mjx-texclass="ORD" transform="translate(1194.7, 0)"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="42" d="M131 622Q124 629 120 631T104 634T61 637H28V683H229H267H346Q423 683 459 678T531 651Q574 627 599 590T624 512Q624 461 583 419T476 360L466 357Q539 348 595 302T651 187Q651 119 600 67T469 3Q456 1 242 0H28V46H61Q103 47 112 49T131 61V622ZM511 513Q511 560 485 594T416 636Q415 636 403 636T371 636T333 637Q266 637 251 636T232 628Q229 624 229 499V374H312L396 375L406 377Q410 378 417 380T442 393T474 417T499 456T511 513ZM537 188Q537 239 509 282T430 336L329 337H229V200V116Q229 57 234 52Q240 47 334 47H383Q425 47 443 53Q486 67 511 104T537 188Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> and C , are attached by light inextensible strings AB and BC . Particles A and B are held at an equal height of 2 m above a horizontal floor. B rests on a rough horizontal surface and when in motion experiences a constant resistive force of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> N. It is given that B does not reach either pulley during any part of the motion following release.<br>
The particles are released and A hits the ground 4 seconds later.<br>
(a) Find the tension in each of the strings AB and BC .</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>To find the tension in the strings AB and BC, we first need to determine the acceleration of the system. Since particle A hits the ground after 4 seconds, we can use the kinematic equation to find the acceleration.</div>
<div>Consider the acceleration on the whole system and then analyze the forces acting on each particle to find the tensions in the strings.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the tension in the strings AB and BC, we first need to determine the acceleration of the system. Since particle A hits the ground after 4 seconds, we can use the kinematic equation to find the acceleration.<br>

<div>Now, we can analyze the forces acting on each particle to find the tensions in the strings.<br>
For tennsion on string AB:<br>

<div>(b) Find the exact value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>To find the value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>, we need to analyze the forces acting on particle B. The tension in string AB and the tension in string BC will help us set up an equation involving <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>. Use Newtons second law to relate these forces and solve for <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.</div>

<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>To find the value of <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>, we need to analyze the forces acting on particle B. <mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.566ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="2.74ex" height="2.262ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -750 1211 1000"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mo"><path data-c="28" d="M94 250Q94 319 104 381T127 488T164 576T202 643T244 695T277 729T302 750H315H319Q333 750 333 741Q333 738 316 720T275 667T226 581T184 443T167 250T184 58T225 -81T274 -167T316 -220T333 -241Q333 -250 318 -250H315H302L274 -226Q180 -141 137 -14T94 250Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mi" transform="translate(389, 0)"><path data-c="63" d="M34 159Q34 268 120 355T306 442Q362 442 394 418T427 355Q427 326 408 306T360 285Q341 285 330 295T319 325T330 359T352 380T366 386H367Q367 388 361 392T340 400T306 404Q276 404 249 390Q228 381 206 359Q162 315 142 235T121 119Q121 73 147 50Q169 26 205 26H209Q321 26 394 111Q403 121 406 121Q410 121 419 112T429 98T420 83T391 55T346 25T282 0T202 -11Q127 -11 81 37T34 159Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(822, 0)"><path data-c="29" d="M60 749L64 750Q69 750 74 750H86L114 726Q208 641 251 514T294 250Q294 182 284 119T261 12T224 -76T186 -143T145 -194T113 -227T90 -246Q87 -249 86 -250H74Q66 -250 63 -250T58 -247T55 -238Q56 -237 66 -225Q221 -64 221 250T66 725Q56 737 55 738Q55 746 60 749Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> Explain how you have used the modelling assumption that the pulleys are smooth.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>The assumption that the pulleys are smooth implies that there is no friction between the string and the pulleys, allowing us to analyze the forces acting on each particle without considering any additional forces due to friction at the pulleys.</div>
</div>
</details>
<br>
<div>The particle A detaches from the string as soon as it hits the floor.<br>
(d) Find the acceleration of the system when C is moving downwards.</div>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:blue">Hint</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px;">
<div>Basically we can treat the question as new system with only particles B and C.<br>
The friction force <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: 0" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.699ex" height="1.545ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -683 751 683"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="50" d="M287 628Q287 635 230 637Q206 637 199 638T192 648Q192 649 194 659Q200 679 203 681T397 683Q587 682 600 680Q664 669 707 631T751 530Q751 453 685 389Q616 321 507 303Q500 302 402 301H307L277 182Q247 66 247 59Q247 55 248 54T255 50T272 48T305 46H336Q342 37 342 35Q342 19 335 5Q330 0 319 0Q316 0 282 1T182 2Q120 2 87 2T51 1Q33 1 33 11Q33 13 36 25Q40 41 44 43T67 46Q94 46 127 49Q141 52 146 61Q149 65 218 339T287 628ZM645 554Q645 567 643 575T634 597T609 619T560 635Q553 636 480 637Q463 637 445 637T416 636T404 636Q391 635 386 627Q384 621 367 550T332 412T314 344Q314 342 395 342H407H430Q542 342 590 392Q617 419 631 471T645 554Z"></path></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span> still acts on particle B, but with different direction.</div>
</div>
</details>
<details>
<summary><span class="details-marker">&nbsp;</span><span style="color:green">Solutions</span></summary><div style="font-size: 22px">
<div>Let the acceleration after A detaches (with C moving downwards taken as positive) be <span class="math-inline ">
<mjx-container class="MathJax" jax="SVG"><svg style="vertical-align: -0.023ex" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="1.75ex" height="1.74ex" role="img" focusable="false" viewBox="0 -759 773.5 769"><g stroke="currentColor" fill="currentColor" stroke-width="0" transform="matrix(1 0 0 -1 0 0)"><g data-mml-node="math"><g data-mml-node="msup"><g data-mml-node="mi"><path data-c="61" d="M33 157Q33 258 109 349T280 441Q331 441 370 392Q386 422 416 422Q429 422 439 414T449 394Q449 381 412 234T374 68Q374 43 381 35T402 26Q411 27 422 35Q443 55 463 131Q469 151 473 152Q475 153 483 153H487Q506 153 506 144Q506 138 501 117T481 63T449 13Q436 0 417 -8Q409 -10 393 -10Q359 -10 336 5T306 36L300 51Q299 52 296 50Q294 48 292 46Q233 -10 172 -10Q117 -10 75 30T33 157ZM351 328Q351 334 346 350T323 385T277 405Q242 405 210 374T160 293Q131 214 119 129Q119 126 119 118T118 106Q118 61 136 44T179 26Q217 26 254 59T298 110Q300 114 325 217T351 328Z"></path></g><g data-mml-node="mo" transform="translate(529, 363) scale(0.707)"><path data-c="2032" d="M79 43Q73 43 52 49T30 61Q30 68 85 293T146 528Q161 560 198 560Q218 560 240 545T262 501Q262 496 260 486Q259 479 173 263T84 45T79 43Z"></path></g></g></g></g></svg></mjx-container></span>.<br>
Consider the whole system of particles B and C, the only forces acting on the system are weight of C and friction P toward left, so we have:</div>
<div><span class="math-block ">

<div>so</div>

<div>Therefore</div>
